	focus = {																							
		id = AFG_take_control_of_the_arms_smuggling_trade
		icon = GFX_z_goal_take_control_of_the_arms_smuggling_trade

		}

			has_country_leader = { character = AFG_Mohammad_Hashim_han ruling_only = yes }

					tooltip = AFG_demilitarize_state_tt 
					check_variable = { AFG_demilitarize_state < 4 }
				}
			}
		}
		completion_reward = {
			log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName] ([Root.GetTag]): Focus AFG_take_control_of_the_arms_smuggling_trade"
			custom_effect_tooltip = AFG_take_control_of_the_arms_smuggling_trade_tt
			every_controlled_state = {
				limit = { check_variable = { AFG_demilitarize_state < 4 } }
				add_to_variable = {
					var = AFG_demilitarize_state
					value = 1
					tooltip = AFG_plus_to_demilitarize_state_tt
				}
				clamp_variable = {
					var = AFG_demilitarize_state
					min = 0
					max = 4
				}
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { AFG_demilitarize_state > 3 } }
					ROOT = {
						add_to_variable = {
							var = AFG_num_of_demilitarized_state
							value = 1
						}
						if = {
							limit = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = AFG_creation_of_the_regular_army } }
							custom_effect_tooltip = AFG_tribes_tension_modifier_tt_1
							add_to_variable = { AFG_training_time_army_factor_var = -0.05 tooltip = training_time_army_factor_tooltip }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = AFG_arms_smuggling }
				custom_effect_tooltip = AFG_hoz_tt
				remove_ideas = AFG_arms_smuggling
			}
		}
	}
